<ALERT_LARGE_CHAR_COL1>select buyer_name ,email_address ,sysdate ,rpad(PO_number,10) || rpad(item_code,30) || rpad(quantity,15)|| rpad(po_qty,15)|| rpad(po_rcvd,15)|| rpad(open_quantity,15)|| rpad(error_message,100) into &p_buyer ,&p_email ,&p_date ,&p_text from ( select ppf.first_name||' '||ppf.last_name buyer_name ,ppf.EMAIL_ADDRESS ,poh.segment1 po_number ,msi.segment2 item_code ,b.quantity ,sum(pll.quantity) po_qty ,sum(pll.quantity_received) po_rcvd ,sum(pll.quantity - pll.quantity_received) open_quantity ,c.error_message from rcv_headers_interface a ,rcv_transactions_interface b ,po_interface_errors c ,mtl_system_items_b msi ,po_headers_all poh ,po_lines_all pol ,per_all_people_f ppf ,po_line_locations_all pll where a.receipt_source_code = 'VENDOR' and a.processing_status_code = 'ERROR' and poh.type_lookup_code = 'STANDARD' and a.header_interface_id = b.header_interface_id and a.header_interface_id = c.interface_header_id and b.po_header_id = poh.po_header_id and poh.po_header_id = pol.po_header_id and b.PO_LINE_ID = pol.po_line_id and pol.item_id = msi.inventory_item_id and msi.organization_id = 554 and poh.agent_id = ppf.person_id and pol.po_line_id = pll.po_line_id and pol.po_line_id in(select distinct po_line_id from po_line_locations_all where quantity > (quantity_received + quantity_accepted + quantity_rejected + quantity_cancelled) and quantity > quantity_billed) group by ppf.first_name||' '||ppf.last_name ,ppf.email_address ,poh.segment1 ,msi.segment2 ,b.quantity ,c.error_message)</ALERT_LARGE_CHAR_COL1>

</Q_XXIBM_ALERT_INFO>

PLL.QUANTITY_RECEIVED),'999,999,999.99') OPEN_QUANTITY ,SUBSTR(C.ERROR_MESSAGE,1,50) ERROR_MESSAGE into &COLUMN_NAME &ERROR_MESSAGE_NAME &TABLE_NAME &PO_NUMBER &RELEASE_NUM &ITEM_CODE &QUANTITY &PO_QTY &PO_RCVD &OPEN_QTY &ERROR_MESSAGE from PO_INTERFACE_ERRORS C ,RCV_HEADERS_INTERFACE a ,RCV_TRANSACTIONS_INTERFACE B ,mtl_system_items_b msi ,PO_HEADERS_ALL POH ,po_releases_all por ,po_lines_all pol ,PER_ALL_PEOPLE_F PPF ,PO_LINE_LOCATIONS_ALL PLL where a.receipt_source_code = 'VENDOR' and a.PROCESSING_STATUS_CODE = 'ERROR' and POH.TYPE_LOOKUP_CODE in('STANDARD','BLANKET') and a.HEADER_INTERFACE_ID = B.HEADER_INTERFACE_ID and a.header_interface_id (+) = c.interface_header_id and b.po_header_id = poh.po_header_id and poh.po_header_id = por.po_header_id and b.po_release_id = por.po_release_id and poh.po_header_id = pol.po_header_id and b.PO_LINE_ID = pol.po_line_id and pol.item_id = msi.inventory_item_id and MSI.ORGANIZATION_ID = 554 and poh.agent_id = ppf.person_id and pol.po_line_id = pll.po_line_id and POR.PO_RELEASE_ID = PLL.PO_RELEASE_ID and trunc(c.last_update_date) = Trunc(sysdate)-1 /*and pol.po_line_id in(select distinct po_line_id from po_line_locations_all where quantity > (quantity_received + quantity_accepted + quantity_rejected + quantity_cancelled) and quantity > quantity_billed) and por.po_release_id in(select distinct po_release_id from po_line_locations_all where QUANTITY > (QUANTITY_RECEIVED + QUANTITY_ACCEPTED + QUANTITY_REJECTED + QUANTITY_CANCELLED) and QUANTITY > QUANTITY_BILLED) */ group by C.COLUMN_NAME, C.ERROR_MESSAGE_NAME, C.TABLE_NAME ,POH.SEGMENT1 ,DECODE(POH.TYPE_LOOKUP_CODE,'STANDARD',null,POR.RELEASE_NUM) ,msi.segment2 ,B.QUANTITY ,c.error_message; </ALERT_LARGE_CHAR_COL1>

<ALERT_LARGE_CHAR_COL1>select INTF.BATCH_ID, INTF.STATUS, INTF.CREAT, INTF.REQUEST_ID, INTF.FILE_NAME, ERR.log_msg3 into &BATCH &STATUS &CREATED_DATE &REQUESTID &FILENAME &ERRORMSG from ( SELECT batch_id, cmrequest, v.status, v.file_name,trunc (created_date) CREAT,count (v.file_name), V.REQUEST_ID from XXABS.XXABS_STAGE_INTF V where TRUNC (V.CREATED_DATE) = TRUNC(SYSDATE) and CMREQUEST = 'XXABSMHINV' and status = 'E' Group by batch_id, cmrequest,v.status, v.file_name,trunc (created_date), REQUEST_ID order by 1,2) INTF, (select l.program_name,l.log_msg3, l.created_date,l.batch_id, L.CM_REQUEST_ID from XXABS.XXABS_ERRORS_LOGGING L,XXABS.XXABS_STAGE_INTF V where trunc(l.created_date) = TRUNC(SYSDATE) and L.CM_REQUEST_ID=V.REQUEST_ID and L.RECORD_TYPE != 'Warning' group by l.log_msg3,l.program_name,l.created_date,l.batch_id, L.CM_REQUEST_ID order by 3) ERR where ERR.CM_REQUEST_ID = INTF.REQUEST_ID; </ALERT_LARGE_CHAR_COL1>

<ALERT_LARGE_CHAR_COL1>select distinct TRIM(INTF.BATCH_ID) BATCH_ID, RPAD(INTF.STATUS,10,' ') STATUS, RPAD(INTF.REQUEST_ID,15,' ') REQUEST_ID, INTF.CREATED_DATE, RPAD(SUBSTR(INTF.FILE_NAME,15,4),10,' ') DO_NUM, RPAD(SUBSTR(ERR.LOG_MSG3,1,50),50,' ') LOG_MSG3 INTO &BATCH_ID &STATS &REQUEST_ID &CREATED_DATE &DO_NUMBER &ERROR_MSG from XXABS.XXABS_STAGE_INTF INTF, XXABS.XXABS_ERRORS_LOGGING ERR WHERE TRUNC(INTF.CREATED_DATE)>=TRUNC(sysdate-1) and INTF.CMREQUEST = 'XXABSISOSHIP' and INTF.REC_TYPE=2 AND TRUNC(ERR.CREATED_DATE) >= TRUNC(sysdate -1) and ERR.PROGRAM_NAME = 'XXABS_ISO_SHIPMENT_PKG' and SUBSTR(INTF.FILE_NAME,15,4) = ERR.DELIVERY_ORDER_NUMBER (+) and intf.STATUS in('E','X',null); </ALERT_LARGE_CHAR_COL1>

</Q_XXIBM_ALERT_INFO>

<ALERT_LARGE_CHAR_COL1>select POH.SEGMENT1, TO_CHAR(POR.RELEASE_NUM,'999,999') RELEASE_NUM, TO_CHAR(PLL.LAST_ACCEPT_DATE,'DD-MON-YY HH24:MI') LAST_ACCEPT_DATE, PLL.ATTRIBUTE10, PLL.ATTRIBUTE11, PLL.ATTRIBUTE15, org.organization_code || '-' || org.organization_name ship_to_org, MTL.SEGMENT1 ||'_'|| MTL.SEGMENT2 ITEMNO, TO_CHAR(PLL.QUANTITY,'999,999,999.99') QUANTITY, TO_CHAR(PLL.QUANTITY_RECEIVED,'999,999,999.99') QUANTITY_RECEIVED, PLL.QUANTITY_ACCEPTED, PLL.QUANTITY_REJECTED, to_char(PLL.QUANTITY_BILLED,'999,999,999.99') quantity_billed, to_char(PLL.QUANTITY_CANCELLED,'999,999,999.99') quantity_cancelled, PLL.UNIT_MEAS_LOOKUP_CODE, PLL.APPROVED_FLAG, to_char(PLL.APPROVED_DATE,'DD-MON-YY HH24:MI') APPROVED_DATE, PLL.CANCEL_FLAG, to_char(PLL.CANCEL_DATE,'DD-MON-YY HH24:MI') CANCEL_DATE, PLL.QTY_RCV_EXCEPTION_CODE, PLL.QTY_RCV_TOLERANCE, PLL.SHIPMENT_TYPE into &PO &RELEASE &ACCEPT_DATE &ATTRIBUTE10 &ATTRIBUTE11 &ATTRIBUTE15 &SHIP_TO_ORG &ITEMNO &QUANTITY &RECEIVED &ACCEPTED &REJECTED &BILLED &CANCELLED &UOM &APPROVED &APPROVED_DATE &CANCEL_FLAG &CANCEL_DATE &RCV_EXCEPTION &RCV_TOLERANCE &SHIPMENT_TYPE from PO_LINE_LOCATIONS_ALL PLL, PO_HEADERS_ALL POH, PO_RELEASES_ALL POR, PO_LINES_ALL POL, MTL_SYSTEM_ITEMS_B MTL, apps.org_organization_definitions org where POH.PO_HEADER_ID = POL.PO_HEADER_ID and POH.PO_HEADER_ID = PLL.PO_HEADER_ID and POL.PO_LINE_ID = PLL.PO_LINE_ID and PLL.PO_RELEASE_ID = POR.PO_RELEASE_ID (+) and POL.ITEM_ID = MTL.INVENTORY_ITEM_ID and PLL.SHIP_TO_ORGANIZATION_ID = MTL.ORGANIZATION_ID and pll.ship_to_organization_id = org.organization_id and PLL.LAST_ACCEPT_DATE is not null and PLL.LAST_ACCEPT_DATE < sysdate and (PLL.QUANTITY_RECEIVED + PLL.QUANTITY_CANCELLED + PLL.QUANTITY_REJECTED) < PLL.QUANTITY and PLL.CLOSED_CODE = 'OPEN' order by segment1, release_num;</ALERT_LARGE_CHAR_COL1>
